## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialize
    Initialize --> ConvertDateTime: eta is datetime
    Initialize --> PreserveNone: eta is None
    Initialize --> PreserveString: eta is string
    ConvertDateTime --> ReturnISODate
    PreserveNone --> ReturnNone
    PreserveString --> ReturnString
    ReturnISODate --> [*]
    ReturnNone --> [*]
    ReturnString --> [*]
```
